    93→            Try Again
    94→          </UButton>
    95→        </div>
    96→
    97→        <!-- Empty state -->
    98→        <div v-else-if="!formattedXml" class="preview-empty no-print">
    99→          <p>Your formatted document will appear here.</p>
   100→        </div>
   101→
   102→        <!-- Preview + review note -->
   103→        <template v-else>
   104→          <PreviewPanel
   105→            :xml-content="formattedXml"
   106→            :zoom="1"
   107→          />
   108→          <div class="review-note no-print">
   109→            Your content has been formatted but not rewritten. Please review before exporting.
   110→          </div>
   111→        </template>
   112→      </div>
   113→    </div>
   114→  </div>
   115→</template>
   116→
   117→<script setup lang="ts">
   118→import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   119→
   120→useHead({
   121→  title: 'OhMyDoc',
   122→})
   123→
   124→const placeholder = `Paste your resume or cover letter here.
   125→
   126→Example:
   127→Jane Smith
   128→jane@email.com · Toronto, ON
   129→
   130→Software Engineer with 8 years...`
   131→
   132→const textContent = ref('')
   133→const formattedXml = ref('')
   134→const isFormatting = ref(false)
   135→const formatError = ref('')
   136→const documentType = ref('')
   137→const divergence = ref(0)
   138→const validationMessage = ref('')
   139→const selectedDocType = ref<'resume' | 'letter'>('resume')
   140→
   141→const formatButtonLabel = computed(() =>
   142→  selectedDocType.value === 'letter' ? 'Format My Letter' : 'Format My Resume',
   143→)
   144→
   145→const showDivergenceWarning = computed(() => formattedXml.value && divergence.value > 0.05)
   146→
   147→function handlePrint() {
   148→  window.print()
   149→}
   150→
   151→async function formatDocument() {
   152→  validationMessage.value = ''
   153→
   154→  if (!textContent.value.trim()) return
   155→
   156→  if (textContent.value.trim().length < 50) {
   157→    validationMessage.value = 'Please paste at least 50 characters of content to format.'
   158→    return

USERMESSAGE #19
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * XML Parser Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides XML parsing functionality using browser's native DOMParser API.
     5→ * Zero dependencies approach for fast, simple XML parsing (DECISIONS.md Decision 6).
     6→ */
     7→
     8→// TypeScript interfaces matching the XML schema from docs/sample/cover-letter.xml
     9→
    10→export interface Address {
    11→  street: string
    12→  city: string
    13→  state: string
    14→  zipCode: string
    15→}
    16→
    17→export interface ContactInformation {
    18→  phone: string
    19→  email: string
    20→}
    21→
    22→export interface Applicant {
    23→  name: string
    24→  address: Address
    25→  contactInformation: ContactInformation
    26→}
    27→
    28→export interface Achievement {
    29→  text: string
    30→}
    31→
    32→export interface Experience {
    33→  employer: string
    34→  achievements: Achievement[]
    35→}
    36→
    37→export interface Letter {
    38→  salutation: string
    39→  introduction: string
    40→  experienceSection: Experience[]
    41→  motivation: string
    42→  closing: string
    43→  signature: string
    44→}
    45→
    46→export interface Recipient {
    47→  position: string
    48→  company: string
    49→  address: Address
    50→}
    51→
    52→export interface ParsedData {
    53→  formatStyle?: string
    54→  applicant: Applicant
    55→  date: string
    56→  recipient: Recipient
    57→  letter: Letter
    58→}
    59→
    60→export interface ValidationResult {
    61→  isValid: boolean
    62→  error?: string
    63→}
    64→
    65→export interface ParseResult {
    66→  success: boolean
    67→  data?: unknown
    68→  error?: string
    69→}
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Helper function to safely extract text content from an XML element
    73→ */
    74→function getTextContent(element: Element | null, tagName: string, parentName: string = 'document'): string {
    75→  if (!element) {
    76→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    77→  }
    78→  const node = element.querySelector(tagName)
    79→  if (!node) {
    80→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    81→  }
    82→  return node.textContent?.trim() || ''
    83→}
    84→
    85→/**
    86→ * Parse address element (reusable for applicant and recipient addresses)
    87→ */
    88→function parseAddress(addressElement: Element | null, context: string): Address {
    89→  if (!addressElement) {
    90→    throw new Error(`Missing address element in ${context}`)
    91→  }
    92→
    93→  return {
    94→    street: getTextContent(addressElement, 'street', `${context} address`),
    95→    city: getTextContent(addressElement, 'city', `${context} address`),
    96→    state: getTextContent(addressElement, 'state', `${context} address`),
    97→    zipCode: getTextContent(addressElement, 'zipCode', `${context} address`),
    98→  }
    99→}
   100→
   101→/**
   102→ * Validate XML for well-formedness and basic schema requirements
   103→ *
   104→ * @param xmlString - XML string to validate
   105→ * @returns ValidationResult with isValid flag and optional error message
   106→ */
   107→export function validateXml(xmlString: string): ValidationResult {
   108→  if (!xmlString || xmlString.trim() === '') {
   109→    return {
   110→      isValid: false,
   111→      error: 'XML input is empty. Please provide valid XML content.',
   112→    }
   113→  }
   114→
   115→  const parser = new DOMParser()
   116→  const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   117→
   118→  // Check for parser errors
   119→  const parserError = xmlDoc.querySelector('parsererror')
   120→  if (parserError) {
   121→    // Extract meaningful error message from parsererror element
   122→    const errorText = parserError.textContent || 'Unknown XML parsing error'
   123→
   124→    // Provide user-friendly error messages for common issues
   125→    if (errorText.includes('unclosed tag') || errorText.includes('Opening and ending tag mismatch')) {
   126→      return {
   127→        isValid: false,
   128→        error: 'XML has unclosed or mismatched tags. Please check that all opening tags have corresponding closing tags.',
   129→      }
   130→    }
   131→    if (errorText.includes('Unexpected end of file') || errorText.includes('premature end of data')) {
   132→      return {
   133→        isValid: false,
   134→        error: 'XML is incomplete. The document appears to end unexpectedly.',
   135→      }
   136→    }
   137→    if (errorText.includes('invalid character') || errorText.includes('not well-formed')) {
   138→      return {
   139→        isValid: false,
   140→        error: 'XML contains invalid characters or syntax. Please check for special characters that need to be escaped.',
   141→      }
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    return {
   145→      isValid: false,
   146→      error: `XML parsing error: ${errorText}`,
   147→    }
   148→  }
   149→
   150→  // Check for root element
   151→  const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   152→  if (!root || root.tagName !== 'applicationDocument') {
   153→    return {
   154→      isValid: false,
   155→      error: 'Invalid XML structure. Root element must be <applicationDocument>.',
   156→    }
   157→  }
   158→
   159→  // Check for required top-level elements
   160→  const requiredElements = ['applicant', 'date', 'recipient', 'letter']
   161→  for (const elementName of requiredElements) {
   162→    if (!root.querySelector(elementName)) {
   163→      return {
   164→        isValid: false,
   165→        error: `Missing required element: <${elementName}>. All application documents must include applicant, date, recipient, and letter sections.`,
   166→      }
   167→    }
   168→  }
   169→
   170→  return { isValid: true }
   171→}
   172→
   173→/**
   174→ * Parse XML string into structured data object
   175→ *
   176→ * @param xmlString - XML string to parse
   177→ * @returns ParseResult with success flag, parsed data, or error message
   178→ */
   179→export function parseXml(xmlString: string): ParseResult {
   180→  try {
   181→    // First validate the XML
   182→    const validation = validateXml(xmlString)
   183→    if (!validation.isValid) {
   184→      return {
   185→        success: false,
   186→        error: validation.error,
   187→      }
   188→    }
   189→
   190→    const parser = new DOMParser()
   191→    const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   192→    const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   193→
   194→    // Extract formatStyle attribute (optional)
   195→    const formatStyle = root.getAttribute('formatStyle') || undefined
   196→
   197→    // Parse applicant section
   198→    const applicantElement = root.querySelector('applicant')
   199→    if (!applicantElement) {
   200→      throw new Error('Missing required element: applicant')
   201→    }
   202→
   203→    const applicant: Applicant = {
   204→      name: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'name', 'applicant'),
   205→      address: parseAddress(applicantElement.querySelector('address'), 'applicant'),
   206→      contactInformation: {
   207→        phone: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation phone', 'applicant'),
   208→        email: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation email', 'applicant'),
   209→      },
   210→    }
   211→
   212→    // Parse date
   213→    const date = getTextContent(root, 'date')
   214→
   215→    // Parse recipient section
   216→    const recipientElement = root.querySelector('recipient')
   217→    if (!recipientElement) {
   218→      throw new Error('Missing required element: recipient')
   219→    }
   220→
   221→    const recipient: Recipient = {
   222→      position: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'position', 'recipient'),
   223→      company: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'company', 'recipient'),
   224→      address: parseAddress(recipientElement.querySelector('address'), 'recipient'),
   225→    }
   226→
   227→    // Parse letter section
   228→    const letterElement = root.querySelector('letter')
   229→    if (!letterElement) {
   230→      throw new Error('Missing required element: letter')
   231→    }
   232→
   233→    // Parse experiences
   234→    const experienceElements = letterElement.querySelectorAll('experienceSection experience')
   235→    const experiences: Experience[] = Array.from(experienceElements).map((expElement) => {
   236→      const employer = expElement.querySelector('employer')?.textContent?.trim() || ''
   237→      const achievementElements = expElement.querySelectorAll('achievements achievement')
   238→      const achievements: Achievement[] = Array.from(achievementElements).map(ach => ({
   239→        text: ach.textContent?.trim() || '',
   240→      }))
   241→
   242→      return {
   243→        employer,
   244→        achievements,
   245→      }
   246→    })
   247→
   248→    const letter: Letter = {
   249→      salutation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'salutation', 'letter'),
   250→      introduction: getTextContent(letterElement, 'introduction', 'letter'),
   251→      experienceSection: experiences,
   252→      motivation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'motivation', 'letter'),
   253→      closing: getTextContent(letterElement, 'closing', 'letter'),
   254→      signature: getTextContent(letterElement, 'signature', 'letter'),
   255→    }
   256→
   257→    const parsedData: ParsedData = {
   258→      formatStyle,
   259→      applicant,
   260→      date,
   261→      recipient,
   262→      letter,
   263→    }
   264→
   265→    return {
   266→      success: true,
   267→      data: parsedData,
   268→    }
   269→  }
   270→  catch (error) {
   271→    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred during parsing'
   272→    return {
   273→      success: false,
   274→      error: `Failed to parse XML: ${errorMessage}`,
   275→    }
   276→  }
   277→}
   278→
   279→/**
   280→ * Composable function to use XML parser in Vue components
   281→ */
   282→export function useXmlParser() {
   283→  return {
   284→    parseXml,
   285→    validateXml,
   286→  }
   287→}
   288→

     1→import { Parser } from 'htmlparser2'
     2→
     3→const RESUME_SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You are a professional document formatter. Convert plain-text resumes into structured XML.
     4→
     5→Use this schema:
     6→<document type="resume">
     7→  <header>
     8→    <name>Full Name</name>
     9→    <contact>
    10→      <email>email@example.com</email>
    11→      <phone>555-000-0000</phone>
    12→      <location>City, State</location>
    13→      <linkedin>linkedin.com/in/username</linkedin>
    14→      <website>portfolio.com</website>
    15→    </contact>
    16→  </header>
    17→  <summary>Professional summary text.</summary>
    18→  <experience>
    19→    <role>
    20→      <title>Job Title</title>
    21→      <company>Company Name</company>
    22→      <period>Month Year – Month Year</period>
    23→      <bullets>
    24→        <bullet>Key achievement or responsibility</bullet>
    25→      </bullets>
    26→    </role>
    27→  </experience>
    28→  <education>
    29→    <degree>Degree Name</degree>
    30→    <school>School Name</school>
    31→    <year>Graduation Year</year>
    32→    <note>Honors or relevant note</note>
    33→  </education>
    34→  <skills>Skill 1, Skill 2, Skill 3</skills>
    35→  <certifications>Cert 1, Cert 2</certifications>
    36→  <projects>Project descriptions</projects>
    37→  <volunteer>Volunteer experience</volunteer>
    38→</document>
    39→
    40→Rules:
    41→- Preserve ALL information from the source text
    42→- Omit empty optional tags
    43→- Output ONLY valid XML — no markdown fences, no explanation`
    44→
    45→const LETTER_SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You are a professional document formatter. Convert plain-text cover letters or letters into structured XML.
    46→
    47→Use this schema:
    48→<document type="cover-letter">
    49→  <header>
    50→    <name>Sender Full Name</name>
    51→    <contact>
    52→      <email>email@example.com</email>
    53→      <phone>555-000-0000</phone>
    54→      <location>City, State</location>
    55→    </contact>
    56→  </header>
    57→  <date>Month Day, Year</date>
    58→  <recipient>
    59→    <name>Recipient Name</name>
    60→    <title>Recipient Title</title>
    61→    <company>Company Name</company>
    62→    <address>City, State</address>
    63→  </recipient>
    64→  <greeting>Dear Hiring Manager,</greeting>
    65→  <body>
    66→    <paragraph>Opening paragraph text.</paragraph>
    67→    <paragraph>Body paragraph text.</paragraph>
    68→    <paragraph>Closing paragraph text.</paragraph>
    69→  </body>
    70→  <closing>Sincerely,</closing>
    71→  <signature>Sender Full Name</signature>
    72→</document>
    73→
    74→Rules:
    75→- Preserve ALL information from the source text
    76→- Split letter body into logical paragraphs
    77→- Omit empty optional tags (e.g. omit <date> if no date found, omit recipient <name> if unknown)
    78→- Output ONLY valid XML — no markdown fences, no explanation`
    79→
    80→interface OpenAIChatResponse {
    81→  choices: Array<{
    82→    message: {
    83→      content: string
    84→    }
    85→  }>
    86→}
    87→
    88→function extractTextFromXml(xmlString: string): string {
    89→  const textParts: string[] = []
    90→  const parser = new Parser({
    91→    ontext(text) {
    92→      textParts.push(text)
    93→    },
    94→  }, { decodeEntities: true })
    95→  parser.write(xmlString)
    96→  parser.end()
    97→  return textParts.join(' ')
    98→}
    99→
   100→function detectDocumentType(xmlString: string): string {
   101→  const match = xmlString.match(/<document[^>]+type="([^"]+)"/)
   102→  return match?.[1] ?? 'resume'
   103→}
   104→
   105→function validateXmlStructure(xmlString: string): boolean {
   106→  let valid = true
   107→  let depth = 0
   108→  const parser = new Parser({
   109→    onerror() {
   110→      valid = false
   111→    },
   112→    onopentag() {
   113→      depth++
   114→    },
   115→    onclosetag() {
   116→      depth--
   117→      if (depth < 0) valid = false
   118→    },
   119→  }, { xmlMode: true })
   120→  parser.write(xmlString)
   121→  parser.end()
   122→  return valid && depth === 0
   123→}
   124→
   125→export default defineEventHandler(async (event) => {
   126→  const body = await readBody(event)
   127→
   128→  if (!body.text || body.text.length < 50) {
   129→    throw createError({ statusCode: 400, message: 'Paste more content to format.' })
   130→  }
   131→
   132→  const config = useRuntimeConfig()
   133→
   134→  if (!config.openaiApiKey) {
   135→    throw createError({ statusCode: 500, message: 'OpenAI API key is not configured.' })
   136→  }
   137→
   138→  const inputLen = body.text.length
   139→
   140→  // Select system prompt based on client-supplied docType; fall back to resume
   141→  const docType: string = body.docType === 'letter' ? 'letter' : 'resume'
   142→  const systemPrompt = docType === 'letter' ? LETTER_SYSTEM_PROMPT : RESUME_SYSTEM_PROMPT
   143→
   144→  const response = await $fetch<OpenAIChatResponse>('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
   145→    method: 'POST',
   146→    headers: {
   147→      'Authorization': `Bearer ${config.openaiApiKey}`,
   148→      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   149→    },
   150→    body: {
   151→      model: 'gpt-4o-mini',
   152→      messages: [
   153→        { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
   154→        { role: 'user', content: body.text },
   155→      ],
   156→      temperature: 0.3,
   157→      max_tokens: 4000,
   158→    },
   159→  })
   160→
   161→  const raw = response.choices[0]?.message?.content ?? ''
   162→
   163→  // Strip markdown fences if present
   164→  const xml = raw
   165→    .replace(/^```(?:xml)?
?/m, '')
   166→    .replace(/
?```$/m, '')
   167→    .trim()
   168→
   169→  if (!validateXmlStructure(xml)) {
   170→    throw createError({ statusCode: 502, message: 'AI returned malformed XML. Please try again.' })
   171→  }
   172→
   173→  const xmlText = extractTextFromXml(xml)
   174→  const xmlTextLen = xmlText.length
   175→  const divergence = Math.abs(inputLen - xmlTextLen) / inputLen
   176→
   177→  const documentType = detectDocumentType(xml)
   178→
   179→  return { xml, divergence, documentType }
   180→})

     1→<template>
     2→  <div class="preview-panel">
     3→    <!-- Error Display -->
     4→    <UAlert
     5→      v-if="error"
     6→      color="red"
     7→      variant="solid"
     8→      title="Rendering Error"
     9→      :description="error"
    10→      icon="i-heroicons-exclamation-triangle"
    11→      class="error-alert"
    12→    />
    13→
    14→    <!-- Document Preview — content is DOMPurify-sanitized before assignment to sanitizedHtml -->
    15→    <!-- eslint-disable vue/no-v-html -->
    16→    <div
    17→      v-else-if="sanitizedHtml"
    18→      class="preview-container document-render"
    19→      :style="containerStyle"
    20→      v-html="sanitizedHtml"
    21→    />
    22→    <!-- eslint-enable vue/no-v-html -->
    23→
    24→    <!-- Placeholder State -->
    25→    <div v-else class="placeholder-state">
    26→      <p>Preparing preview…</p>
    27→    </div>
    28→  </div>
    29→</template>
    30→
    31→<script setup lang="ts">
    32→import { ref, computed, watch } from 'vue'
    33→import './resume-styles.css'
    34→
    35→defineOptions({ name: 'PreviewPanel' })
    36→
    37→interface Props {
    38→  xmlContent: string
    39→  zoom?: number
    40→}
    41→
    42→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), { zoom: 1 })
    43→
    44→const sanitizedHtml = ref<string>('')
    45→const error = ref<string | undefined>(undefined)
    46→
    47→const containerStyle = computed(() => ({
    48→  transform: `scale(${props.zoom})`,
    49→  transformOrigin: 'top left',
    50→}))
    51→
    52→const ALLOWED_TAGS = [
    53→  // Resume elements
    54→  'document', 'header', 'name', 'contact', 'email', 'phone', 'location',
    55→  'linkedin', 'website', 'summary', 'experience', 'role', 'title', 'company',
    56→  'period', 'bullets', 'bullet', 'education', 'degree', 'school', 'year',
    57→  'note', 'skills', 'certifications', 'projects', 'volunteer',
    58→  // Cover-letter elements
    59→  'date', 'recipient', 'greeting', 'body', 'paragraph', 'closing', 'signature',
    60→  // Standard HTML tags DOMPurify allows anyway — kept for section labels
    61→  'section', 'h2', 'p', 'ul', 'li', 'a', 'br', 'strong', 'em',
    62→]
    63→
    64→const ALLOWED_ATTR = ['type', 'href']
    65→
    66→async function updatePreview() {
    67→  error.value = undefined
    68→  sanitizedHtml.value = ''
    69→
    70→  if (!props.xmlContent) return
    71→
    72→  try {
    73→    // DOMPurify is browser-only — import lazily to avoid SSR issues
    74→    const DOMPurify = (await import('dompurify')).default
    75→    const clean = DOMPurify.sanitize(props.xmlContent, {
    76→      ADD_TAGS: ALLOWED_TAGS,
    77→      ADD_ATTR: ALLOWED_ATTR,
    78→      FORCE_BODY: false,
    79→    })
    80→    sanitizedHtml.value = clean
    81→  }
    82→  catch (err) {
    83→    error.value = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Could not render document'
    84→  }
    85→}
    86→
    87→watch(() => props.xmlContent, updatePreview, { immediate: true })
    88→</script>
    89→
    90→<style scoped>
    91→.preview-panel {
    92→  width: 100%;
    93→  height: 100%;
    94→  overflow: auto;
    95→  background-color: var(--color-gray-50);
    96→  padding: 1.5rem 1.25rem;
    97→}
    98→

   100→  margin-bottom: 1rem;
   101→}

    11→ * Design spec:

Excellent! Now let me create a comprehensive report of the findings:

## Codebase Exploration Report

I've thoroughly explored the ohmydoc-v2 codebase to understand the current UI structure and how to implement "Try Resume Sample" and "Try Letter Sample" buttons. Here's my detailed report:

### 1. Main App Page Structure (`pages/index.vue`)

**Current Architecture:**
- Single-page Vue component with a dual-panel layout (grid with 2 columns)
- **Left Panel (Editor)**: 
  - `textarea` for plain-text input (v-model bound to `textContent`)
  - Document type selector with Resume/Letter toggle buttons
  - Format button (label changes based on selected doc type)
  - Validation message display
- **Right Panel (Preview)**:
  - PreviewPanel component showing formatted XML
  - Loading skeleton state while formatting
  - Error state with retry button
  - Empty state placeholder
  - Review note below rendered document

**Key Refs:**
- `textContent` - textarea content (ref)
- `formattedXml` - rendered XML from API (ref)
- `selectedDocType` - 'resume' or 'letter' (ref, default 'resume')
- `isFormatting` - loading state flag (ref)

**Action Flow:**
```
User pastes text → textContent ref → formatDocument() method →
API call (/api/format with docType param) → formattedXml ref →
PreviewPanel renders XML
```

---

### 2. AppHeader Component (`components/AppHeader.vue`)

**Structure:**
- UContainer wrapper (from @nuxt/ui)
- 3-section layout: left-actions, center title, right-actions
- Uses slot-based architecture for extensibility
- Currently, right-actions slot shows Export PDF button and mutation warning

**Note:** The header uses @nuxt/ui slots, making it straightforward to add buttons via the header component.

---

### 3. Sample XML Files

**Location:** `/home/gem/project/public/samples/`

**Available Samples:**
1. **cover-letter.xml** (classic cover letter format)
   - Structure: `<applicationDocument>` root with applicant, date, recipient, letter sections
   - Contains applicant info, contact details, date, recipient details, and letter body with experience sections
   - Used as the main example in the app

2. **resignation-letter.xml** (different schema)
   - Structure: `<resignationLetter>` root (different from cover-letter.xml!)
   - Contains sender, date, recipient, body paragraphs, signature
   - Note: Uses a **different XML schema** than the app expects
   - This is NOT compatible with the current app's XML parser

---

### 4. useXmlParser Composable (`composables/useXmlParser.ts`)

**Key Exports:**
- `parseXml(xmlString)` - Parses and validates XML
- `validateXml(xmlString)` - Returns ValidationResult
- `ParsedData` interface - Typed output structure

**Validation Rules:**
- Root element must be `<applicationDocument>`
- Required elements: applicant, date, recipient, letter
- Returns `ParseResult` with `success` flag, `data`, or `error` message

**Important:** This parser is used for preview rendering AFTER the API returns formatted XML. The app currently doesn't need to parse the sample files; it passes them to the editor as plain text or as pre-formatted XML directly.

---

### 5. FRG-216 Implementation (Document Type Selector)

**Recent Changes (commit f59a5e8):**
- Added Resume/Letter toggle buttons in the action bar
- Button styling: toggle appearance with dark background when active
- Format button label adapts dynamically based on selected type:
  - "Format My Resume" when `selectedDocType === 'resume'`
  - "Format My Letter" when `selectedDocType === 'letter'`

**API Integration:**
- `formatDocument()` passes `docType: selectedDocType.value` to `/api/format`
- Server selects system prompt based on docType:
  - Resume: Uses RESUME_SYSTEM_PROMPT (outputs `<document type="resume">`)
  - Letter: Uses LETTER_SYSTEM_PROMPT (outputs `<document type="cover-letter">`)

**No Database:** The selected docType is purely UI state, not persisted.

---

### 6. XML Editor Integration & Content Setting

**Current Mechanism:**
- Plain textarea element with v-model binding
- `textContent` ref updates on user input or programmatic assignment
- No Monaco editor currently used (plain textarea)
- 300ms debouncing happens server-side via the AI API calls

**How to Programmatically Set Content:**
```typescript
textContent.value = xmlContentAsString
```

This automatically updates the textarea due to v-model binding.

---

### 7. useTemplate.ts Composable

**Current State:**
- Returns only the CoverLetterModern template
- Provides `activeTemplate`, `currentTemplate`, `currentTemplateMetadata`
- Single-template system (not a selector for switching templates at runtime)

**Note:** Templates are for the formatted preview output (how parsed XML renders), not related to the sample loading feature.

---

## Key Patterns for Implementation

### Pattern 1: Adding Buttons to Header
The AppHeader component uses slot-based design. You can add buttons via the `#left-actions` or `#right-actions` slots in `pages/index.vue`.

### Pattern 2: Loading Sample Content
```typescript
// Load cover letter sample
const response = await fetch('/samples/cover-letter.xml')
const xmlText = await response.text()
textContent.value = xmlText
selectedDocType.value = 'letter'
// Auto-trigger format
formatDocument()
```

### Pattern 3: Sample Data Structure
The samples exist in two locations:
- `/public/samples/` - served by the app
- `/docs/sample/` - reference documentation

**Important Discovery:** The current `cover-letter.xml` sample uses the OLD schema (pre-FRG-216) with nested `<experienceSection>` elements. The newer API returns `<document type="cover-letter">` with a flatter structure (header, date, recipient, greeting, body paragraphs, closing, signature).

### Pattern 4: Document Type Association
- Resume samples should trigger `selectedDocType = 'resume'`
- Letter samples should trigger `selectedDocType = 'letter'`
- The docType drives the system prompt selection and AI formatting behavior

---

## Recommended Implementation Approach

**Option 1: Add Buttons to Header (Simplest)**
- Add two small UButton components to the header's left-actions slot
- "Try Resume Sample" and "Try Letter Sample"
- Clicking each button:
  1. Loads the sample XML as plain text into textarea
  2. Sets selectedDocType appropriately
  3. Auto-triggers formatDocument()

**Option 2: Add Buttons to Empty State (Secondary)**

## Critical Notes

1. **No External API Needed for Loading:** Samples are static files in `/public/samples/`, directly accessible via fetch
2. **Auto-Format Trigger:** The `formatDocument()` method exists and can be called programmatically
3. **State Management:** Everything is component-level refs; no Pinia/Vuex (keeps it simple)
4. **Type Safety:** TypeScript interfaces are well-defined for ParsedData and all data structures
5. **UI Framework:** Uses @nuxt/ui components for buttons/inputs, making new UI elements consistent

   117→<script setup lang="ts">
   118→import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   119→
   120→useHead({
   121→  title: 'OhMyDoc',
   122→})
   123→
   124→const placeholder = `Paste your resume or cover letter here.
   125→
   126→Example:
   127→Jane Smith
   128→jane@email.com · Toronto, ON
   129→
   130→Software Engineer with 8 years...`
   131→
   132→const textContent = ref('')
   133→const formattedXml = ref('')
   134→const isFormatting = ref(false)
   135→const formatError = ref('')
   136→const documentType = ref('')
   137→const divergence = ref(0)
   138→const validationMessage = ref('')
   139→const selectedDocType = ref<'resume' | 'letter'>('resume')
   140→
   141→const formatButtonLabel = computed(() =>
   142→  selectedDocType.value === 'letter' ? 'Format My Letter' : 'Format My Resume',
   143→)
   144→
   145→const showDivergenceWarning = computed(() => formattedXml.value && divergence.value > 0.05)
   146→
   147→function handlePrint() {
   148→  window.print()
   149→}
   150→
   151→async function formatDocument() {
   152→  validationMessage.value = ''
   153→
   154→  if (!textContent.value.trim()) return
   155→
   156→  if (textContent.value.trim().length < 50) {
   157→    validationMessage.value = 'Please paste at least 50 characters of content to format.'
   158→    return
   159→  }
   160→
   161→  if (isFormatting.value) return
   162→
   163→  isFormatting.value = true
   164→  formatError.value = ''
   165→  formattedXml.value = ''
   166→  documentType.value = ''
   167→  divergence.value = 0
   168→
   169→  try {
   170→    const result = await $fetch<{ xml: string, divergence: number, documentType: string }>('/api/format', {
   171→      method: 'POST',
   172→      body: { text: textContent.value, docType: selectedDocType.value },
   173→    })
   174→    formattedXml.value = result.xml
   175→    documentType.value = result.documentType
   176→    divergence.value = result.divergence
   177→  }
   178→  catch (err: unknown) {
   179→    const raw = (err as { data?: { rawResponse?: string } })?.data?.rawResponse
   180→    if (raw) {
   181→      console.error('[OhMyDoc] Raw AI response (malformed XML):', raw)
   182→    }
   183→    const message = (err as { data?: { message?: string } })?.data?.message
   184→    formatError.value = message || 'Something went wrong. Please try again.'
   185→  }
   186→  finally {
   187→    isFormatting.value = false
   188→  }
   189→}
   190→</script>

    38→</document>

    40→Rules:

    42→- Omit empty optional tags
    43→- Output ONLY valid XML — no markdown fences, no explanation`

    45→const LETTER_SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You are a professional document formatter. Convert plain-text cover letters or letters into structured XML.

    72→</document>
    73→
    74→Rules:
    75→- Preserve ALL information from the source text
    76→- Split letter body into logical paragraphs
    77→- Omit empty optional tags (e.g. omit <date> if no date found, omit recipient <name> if unknown)
    78→- Output ONLY valid XML — no markdown fences, no explanation`
    79→
    80→interface OpenAIChatResponse {
    81→  choices: Array<{
    82→    message: {
    83→      content: string
    84→    }
    85→  }>
    86→}
    87→
    88→function extractTextFromXml(xmlString: string): string {
    89→  const textParts: string[] = []
    90→  const parser = new Parser({
    91→    ontext(text) {
    92→      textParts.push(text)
    93→    },
    94→  }, { decodeEntities: true })
    95→  parser.write(xmlString)
    96→  parser.end()
    97→  return textParts.join(' ')
    98→}
    99→
   100→function detectDocumentType(xmlString: string): string {
   101→  const match = xmlString.match(/<document[^>]+type="([^"]+)"/)
   102→  return match?.[1] ?? 'resume'
   103→}
   104→
   105→function validateXmlStructure(xmlString: string): boolean {
   106→  let valid = true
   107→  let depth = 0
   108→  const parser = new Parser({
   109→    onerror() {
   110→      valid = false
   111→    },
   112→    onopentag() {
   113→      depth++
   114→    },
   115→    onclosetag() {
   116→      depth--
   117→      if (depth < 0) valid = false
   118→    },
   119→  }, { xmlMode: true })
   120→  parser.write(xmlString)
   121→  parser.end()
   122→  return valid && depth === 0
   123→}
   124→
   125→export default defineEventHandler(async (event) => {
   126→  const body = await readBody(event)
   127→
   128→  if (!body.text || body.text.length < 50) {
   129→    throw createError({ statusCode: 400, message: 'Paste more content to format.' })
   130→  }
   131→
   132→  const config = useRuntimeConfig()
   133→
   134→  if (!config.openaiApiKey) {
   135→    throw createError({ statusCode: 500, message: 'OpenAI API key is not configured.' })
   136→  }
   137→
   138→  const inputLen = body.text.length
   139→
   140→  // Select system prompt based on client-supplied docType; fall back to resume
   141→  const docType: string = body.docType === 'letter' ? 'letter' : 'resume'
   142→  const systemPrompt = docType === 'letter' ? LETTER_SYSTEM_PROMPT : RESUME_SYSTEM_PROMPT
   143→
   144→  const response = await $fetch<OpenAIChatResponse>('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
   145→    method: 'POST',
   146→    headers: {
   147→      'Authorization': `Bearer ${config.openaiApiKey}`,
   148→      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   149→    },
   150→    body: {
   151→      model: 'gpt-4o-mini',
   152→      messages: [
   153→        { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
   154→        { role: 'user', content: body.text },
   155→      ],
   156→      temperature: 0.3,
   157→      max_tokens: 4000,
   158→    },
   159→  })
   160→
   161→  const raw = response.choices[0]?.message?.content ?? ''
   162→
   163→  // Strip markdown fences if present
   164→  const xml = raw
   165→    .replace(/^```(?:xml)?
?/m, '')
   166→    .replace(/
?```$/m, '')
   167→    .trim()
   168→
   169→  if (!validateXmlStructure(xml)) {
   170→    throw createError({ statusCode: 502, message: 'AI returned malformed XML. Please try again.' })
   171→  }
   172→
   173→  const xmlText = extractTextFromXml(xml)
   174→  const xmlTextLen = xmlText.length
   175→  const divergence = Math.abs(inputLen - xmlTextLen) / inputLen
   176→
   177→  const documentType = detectDocumentType(xml)
   178→
   179→  return { xml, divergence, documentType }
   180→})

   134→<script setup lang="ts">
   135→import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   136→
   137→useHead({
   138→  title: 'OhMyDoc',
   139→})
   140→
   141→const placeholder = `Paste your resume or cover letter here.
   142→
   143→Example:
   144→Jane Smith
   145→jane@email.com · Toronto, ON
   146→
   147→Software Engineer with 8 years...`
   148→
   149→const textContent = ref('')
   150→const formattedXml = ref('')
   151→const isFormatting = ref(false)
   152→const formatError = ref('')
   153→const documentType = ref('')
   154→const divergence = ref(0)
   155→const validationMessage = ref('')
   156→const selectedDocType = ref<'resume' | 'letter'>('resume')
   157→
   158→const formatButtonLabel = computed(() =>
   159→  selectedDocType.value === 'letter' ? 'Format My Letter' : 'Format My Resume',
   160→)
   161→
   162→const showDivergenceWarning = computed(() => formattedXml.value && divergence.value > 0.05)
   163→
   164→function handlePrint() {
   165→  window.print()
   166→}
   167→
   168→async function loadSample(type: 'resume' | 'letter') {
   169→  const filename = type === 'resume' ? 'resume-sample.txt' : 'letter-sample.txt'
   170→  const response = await fetch(`/samples/${filename}`)
   171→  const text = await response.text()
   172→  textContent.value = text
   173→  selectedDocType.value = type
   174→  formatDocument()
   175→}
   176→
   177→async function formatDocument() {
   178→  validationMessage.value = ''
   179→
   180→  if (!textContent.value.trim()) return
   181→
   182→  if (textContent.value.trim().length < 50) {
   183→    validationMessage.value = 'Please paste at least 50 characters of content to format.'
   184→    return
   185→  }
   186→
   187→  if (isFormatting.value) return
   188→
   189→  isFormatting.value = true
   190→  formatError.value = ''
   191→  formattedXml.value = ''
   192→  documentType.value = ''
   193→  divergence.value = 0
   194→
   195→  try {
   196→    const result = await $fetch<{ xml: string, divergence: number, documentType: string }>('/api/format', {
   197→      method: 'POST',
   198→      body: { text: textContent.value, docType: selectedDocType.value },
   199→    })
   200→    formattedXml.value = result.xml
   201→    documentType.value = result.documentType
   202→    divergence.value = result.divergence
   203→  }
   204→  catch (err: unknown) {
   205→    const raw = (err as { data?: { rawResponse?: string } })?.data?.rawResponse
   206→    if (raw) {
   207→      console.error('[OhMyDoc] Raw AI response (malformed XML):', raw)
   208→    }
   209→    const message = (err as { data?: { message?: string } })?.data?.message
   210→    formatError.value = message || 'Something went wrong. Please try again.'
   211→  }
   212→  finally {
   213→    isFormatting.value = false
   214→  }
   215→}
   216→</script>

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #118
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `public/samples/resume-sample.txt` — New realistic plain-text resume (Alex Morgan, Senior Software Engineer) - `public/samples/letter-sample.txt` — New realistic plain-text cover letter (Jane Park, Product Designer) - `pages/index.vue` — Added `loadSample()` function, "Try Resume/Letter Sample" buttons in the empty state (right panel), and subtle "Try a sample: Resume · Letter" inline links in the action bar (left panel) ## Key Decisions - Samples are **plain text** (not XML) because the app takes raw text as input and the AI formats it — matching how a real user would paste their content - Two discovery surfaces: prominent buttons in the empty state (first-time visitors) and subtle text links in the action bar (returning users who already have content) - Buttons are disabled during formatting to prevent double-triggers ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-217-try-sample-button` - PR: https://github.com/kimwwk/ohmydoc-using-claude-code-agent/pull/38 - Linear: FRG-217 moved to **Test in Progress**
